   (PSP_4:1)	(PSu _4:1)
   Pañcaviṃśatisāhasrikā Prajñāpāramitā IV	PaQcaviMSati sAhasrikA PrajQApAramitA IV
   atha khalv āyuṣmān subhūtir bhagavantam etad avocat: asatpāramiteyaṃ	aTa Kalu AyuzmAn suBUtiH Bagavantam etat avocat: asat pAramitA iyam
   bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: ākāśāsattāṃ subhūte upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: AkASa asat tAm suBUte upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: samatāpāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: sama tA pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: sarvadharmānupalabdhisamatām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: sarva Darma anupalabDi sama tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: vivekapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: viveka pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: atyantaśūnyatām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: atyanta SUnyatAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: anavamardanīyapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: anavamardanIya pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: sarvadharmānupalabdhitām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: sarva Darma anupalabDi tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: apadapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: apada pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: anāmāśarīratām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: anAma aSarIra tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: ākāśapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: AkASa pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: āśvāsapraśvāsānupalabdhitām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: ASvAsa praSvAsa anupalabDi tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: apravyāhārapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: apravyAhAra pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: vitarkavicārānupalabdhām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: vitarka vicAra anupalabDAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: anāmapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: anAma pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānānupalabdhitām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: vedanA saMjQA saMskAra vijQAna anupalabDi tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: agamanapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: agamana pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: sarvadharmāṇām agamanatām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: sarva DarmANAm agamana tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: asaṃhāryapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: asaMhArya pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: sarvadharmāgrāhyatām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: sarva Darma agrAhya tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: akṣayapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: akzaya pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: sarvadharmāṇām atyantakṣayakṣīṇatām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: sarva DarmANAm atyanta kzaya kzINa tAm upAdAya.

   bhagavān āha: kleśasvabhāvānupalabdhitām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: kleSa svaBAva anupalabDi tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: avyavadānapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: avyavadAna pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
   bhagavān āha: kliṣṭasattvānupalabdhitām upādāya.	BagavAn Aha: klizwa sattva anupalabDi tAm upAdAya.
   subhūtir āha: anupalepapāramiteyaṃ bhagavan yad uta prajñāpāramitā.	suBUtiH Aha: anupalepa pAramitA iyam Bagavan yat uta prajQApAramitA.
